Announces 2025 Financial Outlook</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.55pt">EPS of $0.76&#59; adjusted EPS of $1.34</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.55pt">Full-year adjusted EPS of $5.48</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.55pt">Full-year share repurchases of $1.1 billion </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.55pt">Aviation backlog of $7.8 billion at year-end 2024, up $676 million from year-end 2023</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:12.55pt">2025 full-year EPS outlook of $5.19 to $5.39, full year adjusted EPS outlook of $6.00 to $6.20</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Providence, Rhode Island &#8211; January&#160;22, 2025 &#8211; </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron Inc. (NYSE&#58; TXT) today reported fourth quarter 2024 income from continuing operations of $0.76 per share, as compared to $1.01 per share in the fourth quarter of 2023. Adjusted income from continuing operations, a non-GAAP measure that is defined and reconciled to GAAP in an attachment to this release, was $1.34 per share for the fourth quarter of 2024, compared to $1.60 per share in the fourth quarter of 2023. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Full year 2024 income from continuing operations was $4.34 per share, down from $4.57 in 2023. Full year 2024 adjusted income from continuing operations was $5.48, as compared to $5.59 in 2023. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;While a work stoppage at Textron Aviation impacted our 2024 financial results, we saw strong order activity, aftermarket growth, and continued new product development activities with the announcement of the Gen3 family of light jets,&#8221; said Textron Chairman and CEO Scott C. Donnelly. &#34;At Bell, we made significant progress on FLRAA achieving Milestone B, which launched the Engineering and Manufacturing Development phase of the program.&#34;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Cash Flow</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Net cash provided by operating activities of the manufacturing group for the full year was $1.0 billion.&#160;Manufacturing cash flow before pension contributions, a non-GAAP measure that is defined and reconciled to GAAP in an attachment to this release, totaled $692 million for the full year, down from $931 million in 2023.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the quarter, Textron returned $232 million to shareholders through share repurchases. Full year 2024 share repurchases totaled $1.1 billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Outlook<br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron is forecasting 2025 revenues of approximately $14.7 billion, up from $13.7 billion in 2024. Textron expects full-year 2025 GAAP earnings per share from continuing operations will be in the range of $5.19 to $5.39, or $6.00 to $6.20 on an adjusted basis, which is reconciled to GAAP in an attachment to this release.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company is estimating net cash provided by operating activities of the manufacturing group will be between $1.2 billion and $1.3 billion and manufacturing cash flow before pension contributions, a non-GAAP measure, will be between $800 million and $900 million, with planned pension contributions of about $50 million. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:36pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br>&#34;2024 was a challenging year with a strike at Aviation and difficult end markets in our Industrial segment. Our 2025 outlook of higher revenue and margin reflects a stabilized production line with improved productivity at Textron Aviation, growth across our aerospace and defense businesses driven by new product development, and an improved cost structure at our Industrial segment,&#34; Donnelly concluded.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fourth Quarter Segment Results</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Textron Aviation</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues at Textron Aviation of $1.3 billion were down $242 million from the fourth quarter of 2023, reflecting lower volume and mix of $282 million, which was principally a result of production disruptions related to the strike.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron Aviation delivered 32 jets in the quarter, down from 50 last year, and 38 commercial turboprops, down from 44 last year.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Segment profit was $100 million in the fourth quarter, down $93 million from a year ago, primarily due to lower volume and mix, and manufacturing inefficiencies, which included idle facilities costs and higher costs associated with the labor disruption, resulting from the strike.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron Aviation backlog at the end of the fourth quarter was $7.8 billion, up $219 million from the prior quarter.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Bell</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Bell revenues were $1.1 billion, up $58 million from last year's fourth quarter, reflecting higher military and support program revenues of $67 million, primarily due to higher volume on the FLRAA program, partially offset by lower volume on the V-22 program.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Bell delivered 78 commercial helicopters in the quarter, down from 91 last year. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Segment profit of $110 million was down $8 million from a year ago, primarily driven by mix as lower volume on the V-22 program offset higher volume on the FLRAA program.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Bell backlog at the end of the fourth quarter was $7.5 billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%">Textron Systems</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues at Textron Systems were $311 million, down $3 million from last year's fourth quarter. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment profit of $42 million was up $7 million from last year's fourth quarter. <br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron Systems&#8217; backlog at the end of the fourth quarter was $2.6 billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Industrial</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Industrial revenues were $869 million, down $92 million from last year's fourth quarter, largely reflecting lower volume.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Segment profit of $48 million was down $9 million from the fourth quarter of 2023, reflecting lower volume and mix and inflation, partially offset by manufacturing efficiencies and lower selling and administrative expense, largely due to cost reduction activities.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Textron eAviation</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Textron eAviation segment revenues were $11 million in the fourth quarter of 2024, with a segment loss of $22 million, largely associated with research and development expense on new products.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div 2024. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Restructuring</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">In December, Textron announced a strategic review of its powersports product line within the Industrial segment that resulted in additional restructuring actions as it indefinitely pauses production of powersports products. With these actions, in the fourth quarter, the Company recorded total pre-tax special charges of $53 million and an inventory valuation charge of $38 million to write down production-related powersports inventory. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Conference Call Information</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Textron will host its conference call today, January&#160;22, 2025 at 8&#58;00 a.m. (Eastern) to discuss its results and outlook.  The call will be available via webcast at www.textron.com or by direct dial at (800) 343-1703 in the U.S. or (785) 424-1226 outside of the U.S.&#59; Access Code&#58; 84015.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In addition, the call will be recorded and available for playback beginning at 11&#58;00 a.m. (Eastern) on Wednesday, January&#160;22, 2025 by dialing (800) 839-5125&#59; Access Code&#58; 26683. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">A package containing key data that will be covered on today&#8217;s call can be found in the Investor Relations section of the company&#8217;s website at </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">www.textron.com</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-right:62.95pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:135%">About Textron Inc.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-right:0.7pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:135%">Textron Inc. is a multi-industry company that leverages its global network of aircraft, defense, industrial and finance businesses to provide customers with innovative solutions and services. Textron is known around the world for its powerful brands such as Bell, Cessna, Beechcraft, Hawker, Pipistrel, Jacobsen, Kautex, Lycoming, E-Z-GO, Arctic Cat, and Textron Systems. For more information visit&#58; </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:135%;text-decoration:underline">www.textron.com</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:135%">. </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">###</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:133%">Forward-looking Information</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Certain statements in this release and other oral and written statements made by us from time to time are &#8220;forward-looking statements&#8221; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:2.8pt">We recorded pre-tax special charges under our 2023 restructuring plan of $53 million and $78 million in the three and twelve months ended December 28, 2024, respectively. In December 2024, actions were taken under this plan at the Industrial segment in the Textron Specialized Vehicles business related to an indefinite pause in production of its powersports products. In the fourth quarter of 2024, special charges primarily included contract termination costs of $32 million and severance costs of $20 million. For the full year 2024, special charges included severance costs of $43 million and contract termination costs of $32 million. Pre-tax special charges for the three and twelve months ended December 30, 2023 totaled $126 million, which included $87 million in asset impairment charges related to both fixed and intangible assets within the powersports product line and fixed assets at Kautex, along with $39 million in severance costs.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">TEXTRON INC.</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">Non-GAAP Financial Measures and Outlook</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">(Dollars in millions, except per share amounts)</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We supplement the reporting of our financial information determined under U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) with certain non-GAAP financial measures. These non-GAAP financial measures exclude certain significant items that may not be indicative of, or are unrelated to, results from our ongoing business operations. We believe that these non-GAAP measures may be useful for period-over-period comparisons of underlying business trends and our ongoing business performance, however, they should be used in conjunction with GAAP measures. Our non-GAAP measures should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the related GAAP measures, and other companies may define similarly named measures differently. We encourage investors to review our financial statements and publicly filed reports in their entirety and not to rely on any single financial measure. We utilize the following definitions for the non-GAAP financial measures included in this release and have provided a reconciliation of the GAAP to non-GAAP amounts for each measure&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Segment Profit</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment profit is an important measure used by our chief operating decision maker for evaluating performance and for decision-making purposes. Segment profit for the manufacturing segments excludes the non-service components of pension and postretirement income, net&#59; LIFO inventory provision&#59; intangible asset amortization&#59; interest expense, net for Manufacturing group&#59; certain corporate expenses&#59; gains&#47;losses on major business dispositions&#59; special charges&#59; and the inventory valuation charge to write down production-related powersports inventory. The measurement for the Finance segment includes interest income and expense along with intercompany interest income and expense.</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Adjusted Income from Continuing Operations and Adjusted Diluted Earnings Per Share and Outlook</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted income from continuing operations and adjusted diluted earnings per share exclude LIFO inventory provision, net of tax&#59; intangible asset amortization, net of tax&#59; special charges, net of tax&#59; and gains&#47;losses on major business dispositions, net of tax. LIFO inventory provision is excluded to improve comparability with other companies in our industry who have not elected to use the LIFO inventory costing method. Intangible asset amortization is excluded to improve comparability as the impact of such amortization can vary substantially from company to company depending upon the nature and extent of acquisitions and exclusion of this expense is consistent with the presentation of non-GAAP measures provided by other companies within our industry. Management believes that it is important for investors to understand that these intangible assets were recorded as part of purchase accounting and contribute to revenue generation. We consider items recorded in special charges, such as enterprise-wide restructuring, certain asset impairment charges, and acquisition-related restructuring, integration and transaction costs, to be of a non-recurring nature that is not indicative of ongoing operations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div Outlook</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Manufacturing cash flow before pension contributions adjusts net cash from operating activities (GAAP) for the following&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.64pt">Deducts capital expenditures and includes proceeds from insurance recoveries style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font capital contributions to TFC provided under the Support Agreement and debt agreements as these cash flows are not representative of manufacturing operations&#59;</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:13.64pt">Adds back pension contributions as we consider our pension obligations to be debt-like liabilities. Additionally, these contributions can fluctuate significantly from period to period and we believe that they are not representative of cash used by our manufacturing operations during the period.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Verdana',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">While we believe this measure provides a focus on cash generated from manufacturing operations, before pension contributions, and may be used as an additional relevant measure of liquidity, it does not
